\mbox{\Hypertarget{classMela_a7ed076cbbb4121926e53f56cb4d56bab}\label{classMela_a7ed076cbbb4121926e53f56cb4d56bab}} 
\index{Mela@{Mela}!computeDecayAngles@{computeDecayAngles}}
\index{computeDecayAngles@{computeDecayAngles}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeDecayAngles()}{computeDecayAngles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+Decay\+Angles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{qH,  }\item[{float \&}]{m1,  }\item[{float \&}]{m2,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta1,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta2,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi,  }\item[{float \&}]{costhetastar,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



computes the decay angles for gg -\/$>$ H -\/$>$ ZZ as defined in Figure 1 of \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1001.3396}{\texttt{ ar\+Xiv\+:1001.\+3396}} 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Calls \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_afa81b178917557f2d5440957bbf5f08b}{T\+Util\+::compute\+Angles}} to fully calculate angles 

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_afa81b178917557f2d5440957bbf5f08b}{T\+Util\+::compute\+Angles}} \mbox{\hyperlink{CMakeLists_8txt_a6b1ae378d85121122f2ca9615a03d559}{if}} you would like to calculate the angles through inputting your own 4-\/vectors and quantities rather than through the M\+E\+LA event loop 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
This function requires there to be an input event already defined 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function will edit all values {\itshape inplace}. Every value is technically an output. 

The selection for m1 and m2 are based upon which of the leptons is closer to the z mass. \$m\+\_\+1 \textbackslash{}leq m\+\_\+2\$.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em qH} & The mass of the \char`\"{}\+Higgs\char`\"{} as reconstructed by the constituent 4 leptons \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em m1} & The mass of the first decay particle as reconstructed by 2 of the leptons \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em m2} & The mass of the first decay particle as reconstructed by 2 of the leptons \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta1} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+1)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta2} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+2)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costhetastar} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta$\ast$)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi1} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\+\_\+1\$ \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Mela@{Mela}!computeP@{computeP}}
\index{computeP@{computeP}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeP()}{computeP()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::computeP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{prob,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Constant = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Computes the probability for the probabilities on the decay side of things using the constituent daughter 4 vectors along with any jets that could exist. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a7ed076cbbb4121926e53f56cb4d56bab}{Mela\+::compute\+Decay\+Angles}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
All matrix elements (J\+H\+U\+Gen, M\+C\+FM, or analytic), productions, and processes can be used here 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em prob} & This is the value of the output probability -\/ edited by reference \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em use\+Constant} & This turns on the calculation of a corrective constant to different probabilities through \mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a40221b711597c6c682e2283692255f18}{Mela\+::get\+Constant}}. If you would like the \char`\"{}pure\char`\"{} M\+E\+LA calculation to be run, set use\+Constant to false. By default true. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeP\_selfDspin0()}{computeP\_selfDspin0()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+P\+\_\+self\+Dspin0 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{self\+D\+Hvvcoupl\+\_\+input\mbox{[}n\+Supported\+Higgses\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+H\+V\+V\mbox{]}\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},  }\item[{float \&}]{prob,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Constant = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This is a function that calls \mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a8503608babd744076ebe4f173b519844}{Mela\+::computeP}} with preset quark, gluon, and vector boson couplings for spin 0.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
I (Mohit Srivastav) would personally avoid using this function, as it obfuscates the couplings you are {\itshape  really using }. 

It is always a good idea to set couplings yourself so that you know what you\textquotesingle{}re really doing. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

This is a function that calls \mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a8503608babd744076ebe4f173b519844}{Mela\+::computeP}} with preset quark, gluon, and vector boson couplings for spin 1, but sets default values for Zqq couplings. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a8503608babd744076ebe4f173b519844}{Mela\+::computeP}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__coupl_ga85f5106df0e28980c367be244565621f}{Mela\+::self\+D\+Gggcoupl}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__coupl_ga1f4517c76fb7156a1ae14ed919f7dba5}{Mela\+::self\+D\+Gqqcoupl}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__coupl_ga32c366f920eebdfa928bd46e1b25cf08}{Mela\+::self\+D\+Gvvcoupl}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
I (Mohit Srivastav) would personally avoid using this function, as it obfuscates the couplings you are {\itshape  really using }. 

It is always a good idea to set couplings yourself so that you know what you\textquotesingle{}re really doing. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em self\+D\+Gggcoupl\+\_\+input} & an array corresponding to the couplings of \mbox{\hyperlink{group__coupl_ga85f5106df0e28980c367be244565621f}{Mela\+::self\+D\+Gggcoupl}} (between the \char`\"{}graviton\char`\"{} and gluons) using the indices in \mbox{\hyperlink{TCouplingsBase_8hh}{T\+Couplings\+Base.\+hh}} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em self\+D\+Gvvcoupl\+\_\+input} & an array corresponding to the couplings of \mbox{\hyperlink{group__coupl_ga32c366f920eebdfa928bd46e1b25cf08}{Mela\+::self\+D\+Gvvcoupl}} (between the \char`\"{}graviton\char`\"{} and the W/Z bosons) using the indices in \mbox{\hyperlink{TCouplingsBase_8hh}{T\+Couplings\+Base.\+hh}} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em prob} & This is the value of the output probability -\/ edited by reference \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em use\+Constant} & This turns on the calculation of a corrective constant to different probabilities through \mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a40221b711597c6c682e2283692255f18}{Mela\+::get\+Constant}}. If you would like the \char`\"{}pure\char`\"{} M\+E\+LA calculation to be run, set use\+Constant to false. By default true. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+Prod\+DecP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{prob,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Constant = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



computes the combined production and decay probability, with couplings set beforehand 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The J\+H\+U\+Gen Matrix element is not supported 

The following production modes are supported using the M\+C\+FM Matrix Element (as named in \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a1d885f45cfb17fdc0cb80d0b3dd4f28c}{T\+Var\+::\+Production}}) \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a1d885f45cfb17fdc0cb80d0b3dd4f28ca97ce0d58eebcc5155081864c77b0a19a}{T\+Var\+::\+Had\+\_\+\+WH}} {\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+ProdP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{prob,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Constant = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



computes Production side probabilities using couplings set beforehand 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The M\+C\+FM Matrix element is not supported 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em prob} & This is the value of the output probability -\/ edited by reference \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em use\+Constant} & This turns on the calculation of a corrective constant to different probabilities through \mbox{\hyperlink{classMela_a40221b711597c6c682e2283692255f18}{Mela\+::get\+Constant}}. If you would like the \char`\"{}pure\char`\"{} M\+E\+LA calculation to be run, set use\+Constant to false. By default true. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classMela_a888f07999471870590557aa4fec74caa}\label{classMela_a888f07999471870590557aa4fec74caa}} 
\index{Mela@{Mela}!computeVBFAngles@{computeVBFAngles}}
\index{computeVBFAngles@{computeVBFAngles}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeVBFAngles()}{computeVBFAngles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+V\+B\+F\+Angles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{Q2\+V1,  }\item[{float \&}]{Q2\+V2,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta1,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta2,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi,  }\item[{float \&}]{costhetastar,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



computes the decay angles for Vector Boson Fusion (V\+BF) -\/$>$ H -\/$>$ ZZ as defined in Figure 1 of \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1208.4018}{\texttt{ ar\+Xiv\+:1208.\+4018}} 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Calls \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_ac25514d0b4bfda2daae52ee27f8d2fe8}{T\+Util\+::compute\+V\+B\+F\+Angles}} to fully calculate angles 

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_ac25514d0b4bfda2daae52ee27f8d2fe8}{T\+Util\+::compute\+V\+B\+F\+Angles}} \mbox{\hyperlink{CMakeLists_8txt_a6b1ae378d85121122f2ca9615a03d559}{if}} you would like to calculate the angles through inputting your own 4-\/vectors and quantities rather than through the M\+E\+LA event loop 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
This function requires there to be an input event already defined 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function will edit all values {\itshape inplace}. Every value is technically an output. 

The selection for m1 and m2 are based upon which of the leptons is closer to the z mass. \$m\+\_\+1 \textbackslash{}leq m\+\_\+2\$.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Q2\+V1} & The mass of the first decay particle as reconstructed by 2 of the leptons \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em m2\+V2} & The mass of the first decay particle as reconstructed by 2 of the leptons \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta1} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+1)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta2} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+2)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costhetastar} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta$\ast$)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi1} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\+\_\+1\$ \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classMela_a4b68e6c2c5b1f430d6f88bc048137e88}\label{classMela_a4b68e6c2c5b1f430d6f88bc048137e88}} 
\index{Mela@{Mela}!computeVHAngles@{computeVHAngles}}
\index{computeVHAngles@{computeVHAngles}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{computeVHAngles()}{computeVHAngles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::compute\+V\+H\+Angles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float \&}]{m\+Vstar,  }\item[{float \&}]{mV,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta1,  }\item[{float \&}]{costheta2,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi,  }\item[{float \&}]{costhetastar,  }\item[{float \&}]{Phi1 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



computes the decay angles for Vector Boson Fusion (V\+BF) -\/$>$ H -\/$>$ ZZ as defined in Figure 1 of \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1208.4018}{\texttt{ ar\+Xiv\+:1208.\+4018}} 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Calls \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_a928302e7a9815e5777eeea1fcd832a6e}{T\+Util\+::compute\+V\+H\+Angles}} to fully calculate angles 

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_a928302e7a9815e5777eeea1fcd832a6e}{T\+Util\+::compute\+V\+H\+Angles}} \mbox{\hyperlink{CMakeLists_8txt_a6b1ae378d85121122f2ca9615a03d559}{if}} you would like to calculate the angles through inputting your own 4-\/vectors and quantities rather than through the M\+E\+LA event loop 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
This function requires there to be an input event already defined 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
This function will edit all values {\itshape inplace}. Every value is technically an output. 

The selection for m1 and m2 are based upon which of the leptons is closer to the z mass. \$m\+\_\+1 \textbackslash{}leq m\+\_\+2\$.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em m\+Vstar} & The mass of the virtual Z boson in ZH production \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em mV} & The mass of the Z in decay \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta1} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+1)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costheta2} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+2)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em costhetastar} & \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta$\ast$)\$ \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Phi1} & \$\textbackslash{}phi\+\_\+1\$ \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getMeasurablesRRV()}{getMeasurablesRRV()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structRooSpin_1_1modelMeasurables}{Roo\+Spin\+::model\+Measurables}} Mela\+::get\+Measurables\+R\+RV (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a Roo\+Spin\+::model\+Measureables object containing many observable quantities. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
The parameters in question are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+1)\$
\item \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta\+\_\+2)\$
\item \$\textbackslash{}phi\$
\item mass of the first Z boson (\$\+M\+\_\+\{Z1\}\$)
\item mass of the second Z boson (\$\+M\+\_\+\{Z2\}\$)
\item mass of the full particle (\$\+M\+\_\+\{ZZ\}\$)
\item \$\textbackslash{}cos(\textbackslash{}theta$\ast$)\$
\item \$\textbackslash{}phi\+\_\+1\$
\item Y
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
these angles are defined in Figure 1 of \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1001.3396}{\texttt{ ar\+Xiv\+:1001.\+3396}} as well as (described more generally) in Figure 1 of \href{https://arxiv.org/abs/1208.4018}{\texttt{ ar\+Xiv\+:1208.\+4018}} 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Mela\+::get\+Primary\+Mass (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{ipart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



A function to get the current primary E\+W/\+Q\+CD parameters from M\+E\+LA. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classZZMatrixElement_a8d9f531ff0d8187396b80bd56f3e989d}{Z\+Z\+Matrix\+Element\+::get\+\_\+\+Primary\+Mass}}, which is a Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classTEvtProb_a952ffe128102021e775cb5a6e4a8c48b}{T\+Evt\+Prob\+::\+Get\+Primary\+Mass}}, which calls \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_af0a7eb81fc049eae88e8be0e72e27451}{T\+Util\+::\+Get\+Mass}}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
(Higgs mass/width used in the Matrix Element could be different). Refer to set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Mass\+Width or set\+M\+E\+L\+A\+Higgs\+Mass for explicit references to those.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
You can input negative ids to edit antiparticles (i.\+e. 24 -\/$>$ W+, -\/24 -\/$>$ W-\/) 

In M\+C\+FM both the particle and its antiparticle\textquotesingle{}s mass are changed at the same time. In J\+H\+U\+Gen this is not the case -\/ they are separate entries. 

The particles that you can change when using the M\+C\+FM matrix element are as as follow\+: \tabulinesep=1mm

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double Mela\+::get\+Primary\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{ipart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



A function to get the current primary E\+W/\+Q\+CD parameters from M\+E\+LA. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classZZMatrixElement_a8d9f531ff0d8187396b80bd56f3e989d}{Z\+Z\+Matrix\+Element\+::get\+\_\+\+Primary\+Mass}}, which is a Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classTEvtProb_a952ffe128102021e775cb5a6e4a8c48b}{T\+Evt\+Prob\+::\+Get\+Primary\+Mass}}, which calls \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_af0a7eb81fc049eae88e8be0e72e27451}{T\+Util\+::\+Get\+Mass}}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
(Higgs mass/width used in the Matrix Element could be different). Refer to set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Mass\+Width or set\+M\+E\+L\+A\+Higgs\+Mass for explicit references to those.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
You can input negative ids to edit antiparticles (i.\+e. 24 -\/$>$ W+, -\/24 -\/$>$ W-\/) 

In M\+C\+FM both the particle and its antiparticle\textquotesingle{}s mass are changed at the same time. In J\+H\+U\+Gen this is not the case -\/ they are separate entries.

Resets the event in preparation for the next iteration of the event loop.

\index{resetMass@{resetMass}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resetMass()}{resetMass()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::reset\+Mass (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{inmass,  }\item[{int}]{ipart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Resets the mass for a particle that is an electroweak parameter according to its id. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classZZMatrixElement_aacf31f260e6517938b94975425a69546}{Z\+Z\+Matrix\+Element\+::reset\+\_\+\+Mass}}, which is a wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classTEvtProb_a468300f9b0101f6333dceb0346a7346a}{T\+Evt\+Prob\+::\+Reset\+Mass}}, which is a wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_a51c225f177937798f635f16e7999af99}{T\+Util\+::\+Set\+Mass}} 

This finally interfaces with either the function Set\+Mass in mod\+\_\+parameters.\+F90 for J\+H\+U\+Gen, accessed through .\mbox{\hyperlink{TModParameters_8hh}{T\+Mod\+Parameters.\+hh}} 

in mod\+\_\+parameters.\+F90 the conversion from ipart to the values in J\+H\+U\+Gen\textquotesingle{}s internal code happens with the function \mbox{\hyperlink{TModParameters_8hh_a00e07c5a686985e7a030b7349d0f4998}{convert\+L\+H\+Ereverse(\+Part)}} 

or the masses in the J\+H\+U\+Gen-\/\+M\+C\+FM library at /src/\+Inc/masses.F or at T\+M\+C\+F\+M\+::spinzerohiggs\+\_\+anomcoupl (for t\+Prime and b\+Prime)
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
It is not recommended to use this function to edit the mass of the Higgs in M\+C\+FM. Please use either set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Mass or set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Mass\+Width for that.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}

\index{Mela@{Mela}!resetWidth@{resetWidth}}
\index{resetWidth@{resetWidth}!Mela@{Mela}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resetWidth()}{resetWidth()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::reset\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{inwidth,  }\item[{int}]{ipart }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Resets the width for a particle that is an electroweak parameter according to its id. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classZZMatrixElement_aa0dd3f1dea6bf8642432981e44c013d0}{Z\+Z\+Matrix\+Element\+::reset\+\_\+\+Width}}, which is a wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{classTEvtProb_a8ad3590f69842c1b09ee364ab59e311c}{T\+Evt\+Prob\+::\+Reset\+Width}}, which is a wrapper for \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTUtil_af2f4d9e772c5b03b8554ecbd6778f623}{T\+Util\+::\+Set\+Decay\+Width}} 

This finally interfaces with either the function Set\+Decay\+Width in mod\+\_\+parameters.\+F90 for J\+H\+U\+Gen, accessed through .\mbox{\hyperlink{TModParameters_8hh}{T\+Mod\+Parameters.\+hh}} 

in mod\+\_\+parameters.\+F90 the conversion from ipart to the values in J\+H\+U\+Gen\textquotesingle{}s internal code happens with the function \mbox{\hyperlink{TModParameters_8hh_a00e07c5a686985e7a030b7349d0f4998}{convert\+L\+H\+Ereverse(\+Part)}} 

or the masses in the J\+H\+U\+Gen-\/\+M\+C\+FM library at /src/\+Inc/masses.F or at T\+M\+C\+F\+M\+::spinzerohiggs\+\_\+anomcoupl (for t\+Prime and b\+Prime)
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
It is not recommended to use this function to edit the mass of the Higgs in M\+C\+FM. Please use either set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Width or set\+Mela\+Higgs\+Mass\+Width for that.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
You can input negative ids to edit antiparticles (i.\+e. 24 -\/$>$ W+, -\/24 -\/$>$ W-\/) 

In M\+C\+FM both the particle and its antiparticle\textquotesingle{}s mass are changed at the same time. In J\+H\+U\+Gen this is not the case -\/ they are separate entries. 

The particles that you can change when using the M\+C\+FM matrix element are as as follow\+: \tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{2}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ absolute value of ipart }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Particle Name  }\\\cline{1-2}
\endfirsthead
\hline
\endfoot
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ absolute value of ipart }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Particle Name  }\\\cline{1-2}
\endhead
\PBS\centering 15 &\PBS\centering Tau  \\\cline{1-2}
\PBS\centering 23 &\PBS\centering Z Boson  \\\cline{1-2}
\PBS\centering 24 &\PBS\centering W Boson  \\\cline{1-2}
\PBS\centering 25 &\PBS\centering Higgs Boson  \\\cline{1-2}
\end{longtabu}


The particles that you can change when using the J\+H\+U\+Gen matrix element are as follow\+: \tabulinesep=1mm
\begin{longtabu}spread 0pt [c]{*{3}{|X[-1]}|}
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ ipart }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Particle Name }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Sign Sensitive  }\\\cline{1-3}
\endfirsthead
\hline
\endfoot
\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ ipart }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Particle Name }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ Sign Sensitive  }\\\cline{1-3}
\endhead
\PBS\centering 0 OR 21 &\PBS\centering Gluon &\PBS\centering No  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 1 &\PBS\centering Down Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 2 &\PBS\centering Up Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 3 &\PBS\centering Strange Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 4 &\PBS\centering Charm Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 5 &\PBS\centering Bottom Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 6 &\PBS\centering Top Quark &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 11 &\PBS\centering Electron &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 22 &\PBS\centering Photon &\PBS\centering No  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 23 &\PBS\centering Z Boson &\PBS\centering No  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 24 &\PBS\centering W Boson &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}
\PBS\centering 13 &\PBS\centering Muon &\PBS\centering Yes  \\\cline{1-3}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mela\+::set\+Process (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a0c6d3acf0d4f0af16181b35a88d813a1}{T\+Var\+::\+Process}}}]{my\+Model,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a3d91617913b8024e8b41f4711196815f}{T\+Var\+::\+Matrix\+Element}}}]{my\+ME,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a1d885f45cfb17fdc0cb80d0b3dd4f28c}{T\+Var\+::\+Production}}}]{my\+Production }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the process, matrix element, and production that M\+E\+LA is to use for this event. Calls \mbox{\hyperlink{classZZMatrixElement_a28c78d859931ce874db2ae52a503eb92}{Z\+Z\+Matrix\+Element\+::set\+\_\+\+Process}}, which calls \mbox{\hyperlink{classTEvtProb_afb64507e9e2b613ac14f1fbd07031fd3}{T\+Evt\+Prob\+::\+Set\+Process}}. 

\begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
Remember to set the process for each event, otherwise the M\+E\+LA event loop will throw a segmentation error. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em my\+Model} & a \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar}{T\+Var}} for the Process you would like, as defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a0c6d3acf0d4f0af16181b35a88d813a1}{T\+Var\+::\+Process}} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em my\+ME} & a \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar}{T\+Var}} for the matrix element you would like, as defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a3d91617913b8024e8b41f4711196815f}{T\+Var\+::\+Matrix\+Element}} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em my\+Production} & a \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar}{T\+Var}} for the production mode you would like, as defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceTVar_a1d885f45cfb17fdc0cb80d0b3dd4f28c}{T\+Var\+::\+Production}} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
